# - comments start with #
# - picked words are indented with tab/space
# - rejected words are left unindented with optional " # some explanation" at the end

# selection criteria:
# - simple, nontechnical words (avoid words that are only familiar to high school/college students)
# - nouns, adjectives, verbs, adverbs only (avoid prepositions, conjunctions)
# - avoid loan words (kata serapan)
# - avoid pronouns
# - avoid number words (satu, tiga, sepuluh)
# - avoid conjugated words
# - avoid short words (< 4 characters)
# - avoid words with multiple competing spellings
# - all the above is balanced by the desire to have unique 4-character prefix
